<<if $call is 1>>Mercifully the water is still working. Having taken care of business, you wash your hands and absentmindedly open and close the mirrored medicine cabinet above the sink. It’s empty. But hang on a second, this gives you an idea!<<set $mirror to 1>>\n\n[[Run back to parlor|Parlor]]<<else>>You’re in a bathroom. There’s a tub with [[shower curtain]] drawn at the other end of the room. Above the sink is a [[mirrored medicine cabinet]]. The floor and every other surface are filthy but you can just make out some unusual decorative tiles underfoot.\n\n[[Leave|Corridor]]<<endif>>\n<<mapping>>
You crawl under the table. Suddenly, the floor opens up, and you are falling. There must have been a trap door, you realize just before you hit the concrete, breaking both of your legs. Your screams are loud, but you can still hear the slamming of the trap door above you, and then a second slam—the door to the basement stairs. It is perfectly dark down here now. You scream and scream and scream until eventually you stop, and the house settles back into its silence. \n\n''The End''\n\n[[Undo|Dining Room]]\n[[Restart|Start][state.restart()]]
The kitten isn’t going to be in the medicine cabinet, of course, but you can’t resist looking inside. You press the mirror and the door springs open. There's nothing inside. Perhaps everything was taken away for the murder investigation? You shut the cabinet door.<<set $mirror to 1>>\n\n[[Back|Bathroom]]
You decide to come back tomorrow in the daylight and renew your search. A very wise decision! Unfortunately, just as you reach the sidewalk another branch falls from the oak tree. This one kills you instantly.\n\n''The End''\n\n[[Undo|Front Hall]]\n[[Restart|Start][state.restart()]]
It’s a windy night in October and you’re walking home. At your side swings a cat carrier, from which mewing sounds and a tiny paw periodically emerge. You are the proud owner of an adorable kitten!\n\nYour thoughts are happily occupied with possible names for your new pet as you turn the corner onto your street. But you look up as you pass number 17 and can’t suppress a shudder that has nothing to do with the chilly night. The windows of the house are dark and the place has an abandoned look. The only color comes from the yellow police tape stretched across the door. The whole neighborhood was shaken when five bodies were found here months ago. Details of their deaths were not made public but you’ve heard whispers of gruesome circumstances. The police are still searching for the house’s owner, and it’s generally assumed he must have fled.\n\nHold on, was that movement you saw in one of the windows? You stop to look more closely. Suddenly there’s a loud crack, and a branch from the old oak on the property comes crashing down, narrowly missing you. Startled, you leap out of the way, losing your grip on the cat carrier. It falls to the ground and the door flies open. All you can see is a streak of white as the kitten runs toward the house. \n\n“Wait!” you cry, knowing it won’t do any good. The kitten leaps onto the porch and disappears through a broken window to the right of the front door. What now?\n\n[[Approach house|Front Hall]]\n[[Go home]]
<<if visited() is 1>><<if visited("Corridor") is 0>>The kitten went through the window to the right of the door, so it makes sense to start here. <<endif>>You enter the parlor. Several threadbare chairs and sofas are clustered around a fireplace. You can feel the cool air coming in through the broken panes of the bay window. A large mirror stands at the end of the room. You can just see yourself reflected there through the gloom and dust.\n\n“Here, kitty!” you call again, and listen. But you hear nothing. It’s absolutely silent, unnaturally so, and you have the strange thought that the house is holding its breath.\n\n<<endif>><<if $flashlight is 1>><<if $mirror is 0>>You shine your flashlight around and notice a hole in the wall near the mirror—looks like the ventilation grating fell off. There’s a bookcase the kitten could have climbed to get in there! Maybe it’s in the walls. You hear a scratching sound. It must be the kitten! How on earth are you going to get it out? Will you have to break through the walls? You see yourself in the mirror and are shocked by how pale and frightened you look. Suddenly you feel the need for the bathroom.<<set $call to 1>>\n\n[[Run to the bathroom|Bathroom]]<<else if $mirror is 1>><<if $library is 0 and $call is 0>>You shine your flashlight around and notice a hole in the wall near the mirror—looks like the ventilation grating fell off. Will you have to break through the walls?\n\n<<endif>><<if $library is 0>>Wait a second. Your mind puts the mirror together with the mirrored medicine cabinet you investigated in the bathroom and you wonder if this mirror might open, too. You feel all around it and try to tug it open to no avail. Then you think about how you opened the cabinet and press the frame. There’s a give and the mirror springs open. Behind it is a wooden door with a doorknob. You try it, but it’s locked. There’s a keyhole in the knob. You press your ear to the door and are sure you hear frantic mewing. “I’m coming, kitty!” you say. You need to get through that door. But where are you going to get a key?<<set $library to 1>><<else>>You hear mewing behind the door that you found in the mirror, but it's firmly locked. Where are you going to get a key?<<endif>>\n\n<<if $lockbox is 1>><<if $scrap is 1>>Hang on, what if it’s a key in that lockbox? It looks like it needs a four-digit combination to open. But how are you going to figure it out?\n\nYou pull out the scrap of paper you grabbed from the fridge. Is it really just a simple grocery list?\n\n[img[shoppinglist]]\n\n<<textinput $comb [[Enter four-digit combination|Lockbox]] >>\n\n<<replace "Hint 1">>Hint 1:\nTry saying the items out loud.<<endreplace>>\n<<replace "Hint 2">>Hint 2:\nHow many words in each item? You stand in front of the open mirror door again, shaking the lockbox. You slam it against the wall a few times but it doesn’t open. You need the combination. Suddenly you think of the paper on the fridge in the kitchen. You should probably have checked that out more closely.\n\n[[Go back to the front hall|Front Hall]]\n[[Run straight to the kitchen|Kitchen]]<<endif>>\n<<else>>There must be a key somewhere. Think! The dining room has a [[table and six chairs]], a [[sideboard]] with doors ajar, and not much else.\n\n[[Leave|End of Corridor]]\n<<mapping>>

<<if visited() is 1>>“C’mere, kitty, kitty, kitty!” you call, approaching the house. The porch stairs creak. Of course they do. Reaching around the police tape, you try the door. To your surprise, it swings open. You step through the tape and find yourself in a large entry hall. You try the light switch by the door but it’s not working. Still, as your eyes adjust, you find the streetlights outside allow to see your surroundings. The front hall is dusty but otherwise unremarkable. A corridor runs straight ahead into darkness. To your right is a doorway to what seems to be some kind of living room or parlor.\n\n[[Go down the corridor|Corridor]]\n[[Take the doorway|Parlor]]\n[[Leave the house]]<<else>>You’re back in the front hall, where you first entered. Go into a murder house on a windy night in October? You know there’s no way this ends well. You go home and never see the kitten again. You are a coward and must endure crushing guilt for the rest of your life.\n\n''The End''\n\n[[Undo|Start]]\n[[Restart|Start]]
<<if $lockbox is 0>>You don’t find the kitten in the sideboard, but you notice a small metal box among the few platters and bowls in there. You take it out and try to open it. It’s locked—a four-digit combination. You shake it and can hear something rattling around in there. You try 0000 and 9999, but no luck. You take the lockbox with you.<<set $lockbox to 1>><<else>>You've already taken the lockbox. The cabinet doesn't have anything else of interest.<<endif>>\n\n[[Back|Dining Room]]

You hear a scraping sound below in the darkness and stop halfway down. “Kitty?” you whisper. Behind you, the door slams shut. You scramble to run back up the stairs, but slip and fall backwards. Your head slams down on the concrete floor. As your consciousness fades and your blood spreads in a red halo from your crushed skull, you hear a low, echoing laughter that seems to come from everywhere, and nowhere. Unfortunately, for you, this is \n\n''The End''\n\n[[Undo|End of Corridor]]\n[[Restart|Start][state.restart()]]
The Adventure of the Haunted House
<<if $flashlight is 0>>The kitchen is a total disaster. Junk and dead bugs all over the floor, jars of dark mystery liquids on the shelf, and is that… a chainsaw? You step gingerly over the nasty floor and peek into some cupboards, saying “Here, kitty, kitty,” all the while. The kitten does not seem to be here.\n\nYou are about to leave when you see a flashlight on the counter. Maybe it was left by the police. You grab it and test it: still works. Great! You shine it around but all that happens is you see the dirt and mess more clearly. Then you hear a small sound and look around. There’s a fridge magnet on the floor—it must have fallen. You automatically replace it, and then notice a [[scrap of paper]] held to the [[fridge]] by another magnet.<<set $flashlight to 1>><<else>>The kitchen is a total disaster. <<if visited()==1>>You reach the end of the corridor. There are doorways to your left and right. To the left is what looks like a dining room. To the right you can see a kitchen. You hear a scraping sound behind you and swing around. There’s another door there, open just a crack. You can see stairs disappearing down into the darkness.\n\n“Kitty?” you call softly, but you don’t hear the sound again.<<else>>You’re back at the end of the hall.
